SUB-LIMIT(S) WCDL: < 250.0 MILLION THE AGGREGATE OUTSTANDING OF ALL THE SUB-LIMITS AS PROPOSED ABOVE, SHALL NOT EXCEED THE OVERALL LIMIT FOR THE OVERDRAFT FACILITY. INTERCHANGEABILITY NIL SECURITY UNSECURED MARGINS INVENTORY NOT APPLICABLE BOOK DEBTS NOT APPLICABLE VALIDITY PERIOD OCTOBER 18, 2019 INTEREST PAYABLE MONTHLY IN ARREARS. THE RATE OF INTEREST STIPULATED BY ICICI BANK SHALL BE SUM OF I- MCLR-6M AND "SPREAD" PER ANNUM, SUBJECT TO MINIMUM OF I- MCLR-6M, PLUS APPLICABLE INTEREST TAX OR OTHER STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY, ON THE PRINCIPAL AMOUNT OF THE LOAN REMAINS OUTSTANDING EACH DAY. AS ON DATE THE I-MCLR-6M IS 8.65% AND SPREAD IS 0.90%. ABOVE INTEREST RATE SHALL BE RESET AT THE END OF EVERY 6 MONTHS FROM THE ACCOUNT OPENING DATE/LIMIT SET-UP DATE/RENEWAL DATE AS A SUM OF IMCLR- 6M + "SPREAD", PREVAILING ON THE RESET DATE PLUS APPLICABLE INTEREST TAX OR OTHER STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY. IN CASE THERE IS ANY CHANGE IN THE REGULATORY REQUIREMENTS BY THE REGULATOR APPLICABLE TO THE FACILITY PERTAINING TO PROVISIONING NORMS AND/OR RISK WEIGHTAGE, THEN THE BANK MAY REVISE THE SPREAD TO REFLECT THE REGULATORY CHANGE, SUBJECT TO EXTANT RBI GUIDELINES REPAYMENT THE BORROWER SHALL, UNLESS OTHERWISE AGREED TO BY THE BANK, REPAY TO THE BANK FORTHWITH ON DEMAND SUCH OF THE AMOUNTS AS MAY BE OUTSTANDING AT THE FOOT OF THE RELEVANT ACCOUNT IN RESPECT OF THE OVERDRAFT FACILITY, TOGETHER WITH ALL INTEREST, COSTS, CHARGES. EXPENSES AND MONIES WHATSOEVER STIPULATED IN, OR PAYABLE UNDER, THE FACILITY AGREEMENT AND/OR THE OTHER TRANSACTION DOCUMENTS.
